            <change when="2020-11-04" who="Dominik Wujastyk">Began this file.</change>
            <change when="2023-07-24" who="Deepro Chakraborty">Added 6.65</change>
            <change when="2023-10-23" who="Dominik Wujastyk">Added draft chapters of all
                remaining adhyāyas based on K. Cleaned up the files, removing
                transcription codes.</change>
            <change when="2024-11-27" who="Dominik Wujastyk">Split the uttaratantra files
                from 31-end into 31-44 and 45-66. Updated all the file and folder names
                accordingly.</change>
            <change when="2025-05-30" who="Deepro Chakraborty and Dominik Wujastyk">We
                copied chapter xml:id 6.24 "pratiśyāya" from
                provisional-edition_uttaratantra-01-30.txt to this file,
                provisional-edition_uttaratantra-45-66.txt, between svaropaghāta and krimi
                (xml:id 53 and 54). This is the position of the pratiśyāya chapter in the
                Nepalese MSS.</change>

                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 6.45.1</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         athāto raktapittapratiṣedhaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.45.2"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.45.3"/>

                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 6.45.3x</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         vyāyāmabhārādhyayanavyavoyātapasevanaiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         tīkṣṇoṣṇakṣāralavaṇaiamlaiḥ kaṭvābhir eva ca |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.45.4"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.45.4x">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 6.45.4x</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         abhikṣṇaṃ sevato tūṣṇo rasaḥ pittaṃ pradūṣayet |
                        <caesura/>
                         pittaṃ vidagdhaṃ svaguṇaividahaty āśu śoṇitaṃ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.45.5">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 6.45.5</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tataḥ pravartate raktamūrdhvaṃ cādho dvidhāpi vā |
                        <caesura/>
                         āmāśayād vrajed ūrdhvam adhaḥ pakvāśayād vrajet |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.45.6ab">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 6.45.6ab</label>

                        <caesura/>
                         vāhyāsṛglakṣaṇais tasya saṃkhyā doṣocchritair viduḥ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.45.9">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 6.45.9</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         daurvalyaśvāsakāsajvaravathumadā pāṇḍutādāhamūrcchā
                        <caesura/>
                         bhukte cānne vidāhas tv adhṛtir api sadā hṛdya tulyā ca pīḍā |
                        <caesura/>
                         tṛṣṇākaṇṭhasya bhedaḥ śirasi ca pavanaṃ pūtiniḥ ṣṭhīvanañ ca
                        <caesura/>
                         dveṣo bhakte vipāko viratir api bhaved raktapittopasargāt ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.45.10">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 6.45.10</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         māṃsaprakṣālanābhaṃ kvathitam api yakṛtkardamāñbhonibham vā
                        <caesura/>
                         medaḥ pūyāstikalpaṃ yakṛd iva yadi vā pakvajambūphalābham |
                        <caesura/>
                         yat kṛṣṇaṃ yac ca nīlaṃ bhṛśam atikuṇapaṃ yatra coktā vikārāḥ
                        <caesura/>
                         tad varjyaṃ raktapittaṃ surapatidhanuṣā yac ca tulyaṃ vibhāti
                        ||</l>

                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.46.1">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 6.46.1</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         athāto mūrcchā pratiṣedhaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.46.3">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 6.46.3</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         kṣīṇasya bahudoṣasya viruddhāhārasevinaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         vegāghātād abhīghātād dhīnasatvasya vā punaḥ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.46.4">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 6.46.4</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         karaṇāyataneṣūgrābāhyeṣv abhyantareṣu ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         niviśante yadā doṣās tadā mūrcchati mānavaḥ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.46.5"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.46.6">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 6.46.6</label>
                        <caesura/>

                        <caesura/>
                         tamobhyupaiti sahasā sukhadaḥkhavyapohakṛt |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.46.7">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 6.46.7</label>

                         moho mūrcchati tām āhuḥ ṣaḍvidhā sā ca kīrtyate |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.46.8">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 6.46.8</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         vātādibhiḥ śoṇitena madyena ca viśeṇa ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         ṣaṭsvetāsu ca paittīn tu prabhutvenāvatiṣṭhate |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.46.8.1">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 6.46.8.1</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         hṛtpīḍā jṛmbhaṇaṃ glāniḥ saṃjñādaurbalyam eva ca |
                        <caesura/>

                        <caesura/>
                         pibet surāṃ naiva labheta rogāṃ mano matighnañ ca madan na yātīti
                        ||0||</l>

                    <p xml:id="SS.6.47.trailer">kāyaci ||9</p>

                </div>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.53.9ab">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 6.53.9ab</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         yaḥ śvāsakāsavidhirādita eva coktaṃ śtam cāpy aśeṣam avatārayituṃ
                        yateta || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.53.10">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 6.53.10</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         svaropaghāte nilaje bhaktopari ghṛtaṃ pibet |
                        <caesura/>
                         kāsamardakavārttākumārkavasvarase yutaṃ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.53.11">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 6.53.11</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         siddhaṃ ghṛtaṃ hanty anilaṃ siddhaṃ vārkagale rase |
                        <caesura/>
                         yava<del>ā</del>kṣārājamodābhyāṃ citrakāmalakeṣu vā | </l>

                        <caesura/>

                        <caesura/>

                        <caesura/>

                         mūtraṃ hāridram atha vā saraktaṃ raktam eva vā |
                        <caesura/>
                         kṛcchrāt punaḥ punar jantor uṣṇavātaṃ vadanti taṃ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.58.18">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 6.58.18</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         abhyantare bastimukhe vṛtto lpasthiram eva ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         vedanāvānati sadā mūtramārganirodhakaḥ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.58.19">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 6.58.19</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         jāyate yasya sahasā graṃthir asmarilakṣaṇaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         sa mūtragranthir ity evam ucyate vedanādibhiḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.58.20">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 6.58.20</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         pratyupasthitamūtras tu maithunaṃ yo bhinandati |
                        <caesura/>
                         tasya mūtrayuto retaḥ sahasā saṃpravarttate | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.58.21">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 6.58.21</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         purastād vāpi mūtrasya paścād vāpi kadā canaḥ ||
                        <caesura/>
                         bhasmodakapratīkāśaṃ mūtraśukraṃ tad ucyate || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.58.24">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 6.58.24</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         viśadaṃ pītakaṃ mūtraṃ sadāha bahalaṃ tathā |
                        <caesura/>
                         śuṣkaṃ bhavati yac cāpi rocanācūrṇṇasannibhaṃ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.58.25">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 6.58.25</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         mūtrokasādaṃ tam vidyād rogam pittakṛtam bhiṣak ||
                        <caesura/>
                         picchilaṃ saṃhataṃ śvetaṃ tathā kṛcchraṃ pravarttate | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.58.26">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 6.58.26</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         śuṣkam bhavati yac cāpi śaṃkhacūrṇṇaprapāṇḍuraṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         mūtraukasādaṃ taṃ vidyād rogaṃ dvādaśakaṃ kaphāt || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.58.27">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 6.58.27</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         kaṣāyacūrṇṇasarpīṃṣi kalkāṃ lehāṃ payāṃsi ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         kṣāramadyāsavasvedaṃ bastiṃ cottarasaṃjñitāṃ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.58.28">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 6.58.28</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         vidadhyān matimān tatra samīkṣyāśmarisādhanaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         mūtrodāvartta<del rend="erased">ka</del>yogāṃś ca
                        kārtsnyenehopayojayet | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.58.29">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 6.58.29</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         kalkam ervārubījānām akṣamātraṃ sasaindhavaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         dhānyāmblayuktaṃ pītvaiva mūtrakṛcchrāt pramucyate | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.58.30">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 6.58.30</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         surāṃ sauvarcalavatīṃ mūtrakṛcchrī pibet naraḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         madhuṃ māṃsopadaṃśam vā pibed vāpy atha gauḍikaṃ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.58.31">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 6.58.31</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         pibet kuṃkumakarṣam vā madhūdakasamāyutaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         rātriparyuṣitaṃ prātas tathā sukham avāpnuyāt | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.58.32">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 6.58.32</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         dāḍimāṃmblatāṃ mukhyām elājīrakanāgaraiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         pītvā surāṃ salavaṇāṃ mūtrakṛcchrāt pramucyate | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.58.33">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 6.58.33</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         pṛthakparṇyādivargañ ca mūlaṃ gokṣurakasya ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         ardhaprasthena toyasya pacet kṣīrañ caturguṇaṃ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.58.34">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 6.58.34</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         kṣīrāvaśiṣṭaṃn tatpūtaṃ sarpiṣā saha yojitaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         pibet kṣīran tatas tan tu mūtrakṛcchraharan naraḥ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.58.35">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 6.58.35</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         śakṛt kharasya sampīḍya śakṛd vāpy atha vājinaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         rasasya tasya kuḍavaṃ piben mūtrarujāpahaṃ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.58.36">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 6.58.36</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         mustābhayādevadārumūrvāṇām madhukasya ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         pibed akṣasamaṃ kalkaṃ mūtradoṣanivāraṇaṃ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.58.37">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 6.58.37</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         abhayāmalakākṣāṇāṃ kalkaṃ badarasammitaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         sahāmbhasā salavaṇaṃ piben mūtrarujāpahan | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.58.38">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 6.58.38</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         udumbarasamaṅ kalkaṃ drākṣāyā jalasaṃyutaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         pibet paryuṣitaṃ rātrau śītaṃ mūtrarujāpahaṃ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.58.39">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 6.58.39</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         nidigdhikāyāḥ svarasaṃ pibet kuḍavasaṃmitaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         mūtradoṣaharaṃ kālyam atha vā kṣaudrasaṃyutaṃ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.58.40">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 6.58.40</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         prapīḍyāmalakānāṃ tu rasaṃ kuḍavasaṃmmitaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         pītvāgadībhavej jantur mūtradoṣarujāturuḥ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.58.41">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 6.58.41</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         dhātrīphalarasenaiva sūkṣmelām vā piben naraḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         tasyālābhe suśītena svetataṇḍulavāriṇā | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.58.42">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 6.58.42</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tālasya taruṇam mūlaṃ trapusasya rasaṃ tathā |
                        <caesura/>
                         svetakarkaṭakaś caiva prātas tu payasā pibet | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.58.43">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 6.58.43</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         sritam vā madhuraiḥ kṣīraṃ sarpirmiśram piben naraḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         mūtradoṣaviśudhyarthaṃ śukradoṣaharaṃ śivaṃ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.58.44">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 6.58.44</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         balāśvadaṃṣṭrāṃ krauñcāsthikokilākṣakataṇḍulāṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         śataparvakamūlañ ca devadāru sacitraṃkaṃ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.58.45">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 6.58.45</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         akṣabījañ ca surayā kalkīkṛtya piben naraḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         mūtradoṣaviśuddhyarthaṃ tathaivāśmaribhedanaṃ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.58.46">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 6.58.46</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         pāṭalākṣaram āhṛtya saptakṛtvaḥ parisrutaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         pibet mūtravikāraghnaṃ saṃsṛṣṭan tailamātrayeti || ❈ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.59.1">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 6.59.1</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         athāto mūtrāghātapratiṣedhaṃ vyāvyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.59.1.1">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 6.59.1.1</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         yadā mūtrayato jantoḥ mūtravego vihanyate |
                        <caesura/>
                         mūtrāghātaṃ vadanty etam aṣṭadhā sa tu vakṣyate | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.59.2"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.59.3">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 6.59.3</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         vātena pittena kaphena sarvais tathābhighātaiḥ śakṛdaśmaribhyāṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         tathāparaḥ śarkarayā sukaṣṭo mūtropaghātaḥ paṭhito ṣṭamas tu<del
                            rend="crossed out">ḥ</del> | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.59.4">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 6.59.4</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         alpam alpaṃ bhṛśaṃpīḍya muṣkamehanabastibhiḥ
                        <caesura/>
                         saṃtudyamānaḥ kṛcchreṇa vātāghātena mehate || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.59.5">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 6.59.5</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         pītam vāpy atha vā raktaṃ muṣkamehanabastibhir
                        <caesura/>
                         agnineva ca dahṛmbhiḥ pittāghātena mehate || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.59.6">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 6.59.6</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         samunnaddhodaraḥ kṛcchrān muṣkamehanabastibhiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         saṃhṛṣṭaromā gurubhiḥ śleṣmāghātena mehate || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.59.7">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 6.59.7</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         dāhaśītarujāviṣṭo nānāvarṇṇam muhur muhus
                        <caesura/>
                         tāmyamānaḥ sa kṛcchreṇa sannipātena mehate || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.59.8">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 6.59.8</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         mūtravāhiṣu śalyena kṣateṣv abhihateṣu vā |
                        <caesura/>
                         srotaḥsu mūtrāghātas tu jāyate bhṛṣadāruṇaḥ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.59.9">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 6.59.9</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         vātāghātena liṅgāni tasya tulyāni nirddiśet ||
                        <caesura/>
                         śakṛtas tu pratīghātād vāyur viguṇatāṃ gataḥ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.59.10">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 6.59.10</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         sādhmānañ ca samūlañ ca mūtrasaṅgaṃ karoti ca ||
                        <caesura/>
                         aśmarīsambhavasyoktaṃ mūtraghātasya lakṣaṇaṃ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.59.11">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 6.59.11</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         aśmarī śarkarā caiva śṛṇu kīrttayato mamaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         śarkarāyā viśeṣan tu śṛṇu kīrttayato mama | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.59.12">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 6.59.12</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         pacyamānaṃ tu pittena śoṣyamānan tu vāyunā |
                        <caesura/>
                         śleṣmaṇā veṣṭitaṃ cūrṇṇaṃ śarkarety abhisañjñitaṃ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.59.13">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 6.59.13</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         hṛtpīḍā vepathuḥ śūlaḥ kukṣāv agniś ca durbalaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         tābhir bhavati mūrcchā ca mūtrāghātaś ca dāruṇaḥ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.59.13i">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 6.59.13i</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         ataḥ paraṃ pravakṣyāmi mūtrāghātacikitsitaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         kāryaṃ bhaved yathā yac ca śṛṇu kīrttayato mama ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.59.13ii">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 6.59.13ii</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         kaṣāyāny tha kalkāś ca lehāḥ svedās tathaiva ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         hitā syur mūtraghāteṣu tathaivottarabastayaḥ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.59.13iii">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 6.59.13iii</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         ervvārubījakalkaḥ syāc chlakṣṇapiṣṭaukṣasammitaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         dhānyāmlbapeyo lavaṇo mūtrāghātena pīḍitaḥ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.59.13iv">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 6.59.13iv</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         surāṃ sauvarcalavatīm pradhānāṃ prapiben naraḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         jīrṇṇabhuktaḥ sadā bhuñjaṃ saguḍaṃ śāntim arcchati |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.59.13v">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 6.59.13v</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         madhūdakena saṃloḍya karṣaṃ kuṃkumakasya vā |
                        <caesura/>
                         rātrau paryuṣitam pūtaṃ piben mūtrarujāpahaṃ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.59.13vi">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 6.59.13vi</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         dāḍimāṃmblayutaṃ madyaṃ śuṇṭhījīrakasaṃyutaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         pītvā surāṃ salavaṇāṃ mūtrakṛcchrāt pramucyate |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.59.13vii">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 6.59.13vii</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         pṛthakparṇyādivargañ ca svadaṃṣṭrāñ caiva tatsamaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         ardhaprasthena dugdhasya paced ardhāḍhakodake |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.59.13viii">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 6.59.13viii</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         kṣīrāvaśiṣṭam āhṛtya pūtaṃ sarpir vidhūpitaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         śītīkṛtaṃ pibed enaṃ mūtrakṛcchraharan naraḥ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.59.13ix">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 6.59.13ix</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         gardasya śakṛd vāpi vājināṃ vā gavāṃ tathā |
                        <caesura/>
                         rasasya tasya kuḍavaṃ piben mūtrarujāpahaṃ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.59.13x">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 6.59.13x</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         haridrāṃ madhukaṃ mūrvāṃ mustakaṃ devadāru ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         pibed akṣasamāṃ kalkāṃ payasā mūtrapīḍitaḥ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.59.13xi">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 6.59.13xi</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         triphalāṃ śūkṣmapiṣṭaṃ vā kalkaṃ badarasammitaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         vāriṇā lavaṇīkṛtya piben mūtrarujāpahaṃ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.59.13xii">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 6.59.13xii</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         drākṣārasasya kuḍavaṃ piben mūtrarujāharaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         nidigdhikāyāḥ svarasaṃ pūtaṃ kuḍavasammitaṃ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.59.13xiii">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 6.59.13xiii</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         mūtradoṣaharam pītvā naraḥ sampadyate sukhī ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.59.13xiv">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 6.59.13xiv</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         prapīḍyāmalakānām vā rasaṃ kuḍavasammitaṃ |
                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.59.13xv">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 6.59.13xv</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         mūtradoṣe pibed vāpi hiṃgvelāpānasaṃyutā |
                        <caesura/>
                         pānālābhe hitam vāpi svetataṇḍudhāvanaṃ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.59.13xvi">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 6.59.13xvi</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         elāhiṃguyutaṃ kṣīraṃ sarpirmiśram piben naraḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         mūtradoṣo viśudhyarthaṃ śukradoṣaharañ ca tat |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.59.13xvii">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 6.59.13xvii</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         palāśakṣāram āhṛtya saptakṛtvāpariśrutaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         pāyayet tailasaṃsṛṣṭaṃ mūtradoṣeṇa pīḍitaṃ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.59.13xviii">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 6.59.13xviii</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         adhyardhaprasṛtaṃ vāpi tathā sa labhate sukhaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         pāṭalīkṣāram āhṛtya palāśakṣāravac ca taṃ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.59.13xix">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 6.59.13xix</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         vilvasiṃhīyavanāḍaṃ palāśaḥ pāribhadrakaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         eṣāṃ kṣāram parisrāvya surayā saha saṃsṛjet ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.59.13xx">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 6.59.13xx</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tatra kalkān imāṃ dadyād badarāsthisamanvitāṃ ||
                        <caesura/>
                         varāṃgamūṣakāṇy elā ślakṣṇaṃ dṛśadi pīṣayet |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.59.13xxi">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 6.59.13xxi</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         ekatraitat samāloḍya pibec charkarayā saha |
                        <caesura/>
                         eteṣv eva pacet sarpis taṃ lihen madhunā saha |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.59.13xxii">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 6.59.13xxii</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         saguḍakṣārasaṃyuktaṃ mūtrakṛcchrāt pramucyate ||
                        <caesura/>
                         etat sarvaṃ prayoktavyaṃ mūtrāghāte vijānatā ||</l>

                    <ab corresp="#SS.6.60.2" type="apparatus">
                        <list type="Notes">
                            <item xml:lang="en" corresp="#SS.6.60.2-n1"> One of the only two places in
                                the Nepalese version where this
                                    <foreign>yathovāca</foreign> phrase appears. The other
                                is Suśrutasaṃhitā 5.1.2. At that location, a scribe of
                                witness H added the marginal phrase <foreign>atha khalu
                                    vatsasuśrutaḥ</foreign>.</item>
                        </list>

                <div n="65" type="adhyāya">

                    <head xml:lang="en">[Adhyāya 65: draft edition based on MS K]</head>

                    <head>[Adhyāya 65]</head>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.65.1">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 6.65.1</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         athātas tantrayuktyuddeśaṃ nāmādhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.65.3">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 6.65.3</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tatra dvātriṃśat tantrayuktayo bhavanti |
                        <caesura/>
                         tad yathā | adhikaraṇam | yogaḥ | padārthaḥ | hetvarthaḥ |
                        uddeśaḥ | nirdeśaḥ | upadeśaḥ | apadeśaḥ | pradeśaḥ | atideśaḥ |
                        apavargaḥ | vākyaśeṣaḥ | arthāpattiḥ | viparyayaḥ | prasaṅgaḥ |
                        ekāntaḥ | anekāntaḥ | pūrvapakṣaḥ | nirṇṇayaḥ | anumatam |
                        vidhānam | anāgatāpekṣaṇam | atikrāntāpekṣaṇaṃ | saṃśayaḥ |
                        vyākhyānam | svasaṃjñā | nirvacanam | nidarśanam | niyogaḥ |
                        vikalpaḥ | samuccayaḥ | ūhyam iti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.65.4">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 6.65.4</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         atrāha | āsāṃ yuktīnāṃ kiṃ prayojanam | ucyate | vākyayojanam
                        arthayojanañ ca || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.65.5">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 6.65.5</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         ślokau cātra bhavataḥ ||
                        <caesura/>
                         asadvādiprayuktānāṃ<anchor n="SS.6.65.5-n1"/> śabdānāṃ
                        pratiṣedhanam |
                        <caesura/>
                         svavākyasiddhir api ca kriyate tantrayuktibhiḥ || </l>

                    <ab corresp="#SS.6.65.5" type="apparatus">
                        <list type="Note">
                            <item xml:lang="en" corresp="#SS.6.65.5-n1">We have adopted the vulgate
                                reading here, although it is highly unlikely to be
                                original. In MS H, this pāda appears to read <foreign
                                    xml:lang="sa">asadaprayuktānāñ ca</foreign>. This is
                                unmetrical, the compound is unusual, and there is an
                                unexplained <foreign xml:lang="sa">ca</foreign>. There
                                have been interventions in MS K by a second hand, and also
                                there is a hole in the manuscript just at this point. The
                                ante correctionem reading of K is unclear but appears to
                                be closer to the reading of H than to the vulgate reading.
                                These factors make it hard to reconstruct what a plausible
                                and correct older reading might have been. For the impact
                                on the meaning of this text, see notes to the
                                translation.</item>
                        </list>
                    </ab>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.65.6">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 6.65.6</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         vyatyāsoktās tu ye hy arthā līnā ye cāpy anirmalāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         leśoktā ye ca kecit syus teṣāñ cāpi prasādhanam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.65.7"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.65.8">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 6.65.8</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tatra yam artham adhikṛtyocyate tad adhikaraṇam | yathā rasaṃ
                        doṣaṃ vā || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.65.9">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 6.65.9</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         yena vākyaṃ yujyate sa yogaḥ | yathā vyatyāsenoktānāṃ
                        sannikṛṣṭaviprakṛṣṭānāṃ padārthānām ekīkaraṇam ||<anchor
                            n="#SS.6.65.9-n1"/>
                        <caesura/>
                         tailaṃ pibec cāmṛtavalli<pc> </pc><app>
                            <lem>nimba</lem>
                            <rdg wit="#JKT">vilva</rdg>
                        </app><pc> </pc><app>
                            <lem>haṃsāhvayā</lem>
                            <rdg wit="#JKT">hiṃsrābhayā</rdg>
                        </app><pc> </pc>vṛkṣakapippalībhiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         siddhaṃ balābhyāñ ca sadevadāru hitāya nityaṃ galagaṇḍaroge
                            ||<anchor n="SS.6.65.9-n2"/>
                        <caesura/>
                         siddhaṃ pibed iti prathamaṃ vaktavye <app>
                            <lem>dvitīye pāde</lem>
                            <rdg wit="#JKT">tṛtīyapāde</rdg>
                        </app>
                        <app>
                            <lem>siddhaṃ</lem>
                            <rdg wit="#JKT">siddham iti</rdg>
                        </app> prayuktam |
                        <caesura/>
                         evan dūrasthānām api padārthānām ekīkaraṇaṃ yogaḥ || </l>

                    <ab corresp="#SS.6.65.9" type="apparatus">
                        <list type="Note">
                            <item xml:lang="en" corresp="#SS.6.65.9-n1">The sentence, <foreign>yathā...
                                    ekīkaraṇam </foreign>, does not appear in the vulgate
                                but an almost identical reading appears in Ḍalhana's
                                commentary on this section.</item>
                        </list>
                        <list type="Testimonia">

                            <item xml:lang="en" corresp="#SS.6.65.9-n2">
                                <ref
                                    target="https://saktumiva.org/wiki/wujastyk/susrutasamhita/04-su.ci-1-20/provisional-edition_cikitsasthana_01-20?upama_scroll=SS.4.18.47"
                                        ><foreign>Suśrutasaṃhitā 4.18.47</foreign></ref>.
                                For this section in the <foreign>Cikitsāsthāna</foreign>
                                there is only one witness viz., H, in the Nepalese
                                version. It has a minor variant reading in the second
                                line. Instead of <foreign>siddhaṃ balābhyāṃ ca
                                    sadevadāru</foreign>, it reads <foreign>siddhaṃ
                                    balābhyāṃ sahadevadāru</foreign>. The variant reading
                                in the vulgate as <foreign>°hiṃsrābhayā°</foreign> instead
                                of <foreign>haṃsāhvayā</foreign> is not found in the
                                actual occurrence of the verse in the
                                    <foreign>Cikitsāsthāna</foreign>, where it is
                                identical with its reading of the
                                    <foreign>tantrayukti</foreign> section in the Nepalese
                                version. The following quote from Vṛnda's
                                    <title>Siddhayoga</title> also supports the reading of
                                the Nepalese recension and the reading in the
                                    <foreign>Citkitsāsthāna</foreign> of the vulgate.
                                    <emph>Siddhayoga</emph>
                                <ref
                                    target="https://archive.org/details/VrndaMadhava1894/page/n171/mode/1up?view=theater"
                                    >41.10</ref>: <foreign>tailaṃ pibec
                                    cāmṛtavallinimbahaṃsāhvayāvṛkṣakapippalībhiḥ | siddhaṃ
                                    balābhyāṃ ca sadevadāru hitāya nityaṃ galagaṇḍaroge
                                    ||</foreign>
                            </item>
                        </list>
                    </ab>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.65.10">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 6.65.10</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         yo 'rtho 'bhihitaḥ sūtre pade<anchor n="SS.6.65.10-n1"/> vā sa
                        padārthaḥ | <app>
                            <lem>padasya padayoḥ padānāṃ vā yo 'rthaḥ sa padārthaḥ |</lem>
                            <rdg wit="#JKT"/>
                        </app> aparimitāś ca padārthāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         yatra tu sneha<pc> </pc><app>
                            <lem>svedābhyañjaneṣu</lem>
                            <rdg wit="#JKT">svedāñjaneṣu nirddiṣṭeṣu</rdg>
                        </app> dvayos trayāṇāṃ vārthānām upapattir dṛśyate tatra yo 'rthaḥ
                            pūrvāparayoga<pc> </pc>siddho bhavati <app>
                            <lem>|</lem>
                            <rdg wit="#JKT">sa grahītavyaḥ |</rdg>
                        </app> yathā vedotpattim adhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāma ity ukte sandihyate
                        buddhiḥ katamasya vedasyotpattiṃ <app>
                            <lem>vakṣyati</lem>
                            <rdg wit="#JKT">vivakṣur iti</rdg>
                        </app> | <app>
                            <lem>sāmavedādayaś ca</lem>
                            <rdg wit="#JKT">ṛgvedādayas tu</rdg>
                        </app> vedāḥ | <app>
                            <lem>pūrvāparam upalakṣya</lem>
                            <rdg wit="#JKT">pūrvāpara<pc> </pc>yogam upalabhya</rdg>
                        </app>
                        <app>
                            <lem>vinda vida</lem>
                            <rdg wit="#JKT">vid vicāraṇe vid vindati</rdg>
                        </app> ity etayoś ca dhātvor <app>
                            <lem>ekārthaḥ</lem>

                        </app> | paścāt <app>
                            <lem>padam</lem>
                            <rdg wit="#JKT">pratipattir</rdg>
                        </app> bhavati āyurvedotpattim ayaṃ vivakṣur iti <app>
                            <lem>eṣa</lem>
                            <rdg wit="#JKT">evaṃ</rdg>
                        </app> padārthaḥ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.65.21">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 6.65.21</label>

                         yady asya prātilomyaṃ tad viparyayaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         yathā kṛśolpaprāṇabhīravo duścikitsyā ity ukte viparītaṃ gṛhyate
                        dṛḍhādayaḥ sucikitsyā iti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.65.22">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 6.65.22</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         prakaraṇāntareṇa samānaḥ prasaṅgaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         yathādhikaraṇāntarito yo 'rtho 'sakṛd asakṛd uktaḥ samāpyate
                        sarvatra || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.65.23">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 6.65.23</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         yad avadhāraṇenocyate sa ekāntaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         yathā trivṛtā virecayati madanaphalaṃ vāmayati || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.65.24">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 6.65.24</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         kvacit tathā kvacid anyathā so 'nekāntaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         yathā kecid ācāryā bruvate dravyam pradhānaṃ kecid rasāḥ kecid
                        vīryaṃ kecid vipāka iti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.65.25">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 6.65.25</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         yas tu niḥsaṃśayam abhidhīyate sa pūrvapakṣaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         yathā kathaṃ vātanimittāś catvāraḥ pramehā asādhyā bhavanti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.65.26">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 6.65.26</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tasyottaraṃ nirṇṇayaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         yathā śarīraṃ prapīḍya praścyotayitvādho gatvā
                        vasāmedomajjānuviddhaṃ mūtraṃ sṛjati evam asādhyā vātajāḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.65.28">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 6.65.28</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         paramatam apratiṣiddham anumatam |
                        <caesura/>
                         yathā yo brūyāt ṣaḍ rasā iti vādī tac ca prati
                        pratipādyānumanyate kathaṃcit tad anumatan nāma || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.65.29">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 6.65.29</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         prakaraṇānupūrvyād abhihitaṃ vidhānam |
                        <caesura/>
                         yathā sakthimarmāṇy ekādaśa prakaraṇānupūrvyābhihitāni || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.65.30">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 6.65.30</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         evaṃ vakṣyatīty anāgatāpekṣaṇam |
                        <caesura/>
                         yathā ślokasthāne brūyāc cikitsyeṣu vakṣyāmīti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.65.31">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 6.65.31</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         ity uktam ity atikrāntāpekṣaṇam |
                        <caesura/>
                         yathā cikitsiteṣu brūyāt, ślokasthāne yad abhihitam iti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.65.32">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 6.65.32</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         ubhayahetunidarśanaṃ saṃśayaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         yathā talahṛdayaghātaḥ prāṇaharaḥ pāṇipādacchedanam aprāṇaharam
                        || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.65.33">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 6.65.33</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tatrātiśayopavarṇanaṃ vyākhyānam |
                        <caesura/>
                         yatheha pañcaviṃśakaḥ puruṣo vyākhyāyate | tathā nānyeṣv
                        āyurvedatantreṣu bhūtādiṃ pratyāra<sic>bdhaṃś cintā</sic> iti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.65.34">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 6.65.34</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         anyaśāstrāsāmānyā svasaṃjñā | sveṣu tantreṣu saṃjñā yā sā
                        svasañjñā |
                        <caesura/>
                         yatheha śāstre mithunam iti madhusarpiṣor grahaṇaṃ trivṛtam iti
                        sarpistailavasām || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.65.35">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 6.65.35</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         lokaprathitam udāharaṇaṃ nirvacanam | yathoṣṇabhayāc chāyām
                        anusarati || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.65.36">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 6.65.36</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         dṛṣṭāntavyaktir nidarśanam | yathā agnir vāyusahitaḥ kakṣe
                        'bhivṛddhiṃ gacchati tathā vātapittakaphaduṣṭo vraṇo 'bhivṛddhiṃ
                        gacchatīti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.65.37">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 6.65.37</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         idam eveti niyogaḥ | yathā pathyam eva bhoktavyam iti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.65.39">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 6.65.39</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         idaṃ cedañ ceti vikalpaḥ | yathā māṃsavarge eṇahariṇalāvatittirāḥ
                        pradhānā iti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.65.38">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 6.65.38</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         saṃkṣepavacanaṃ samuccayaḥ | yathā rasodanaḥ kṣīrodaṇaḥ saghṛtā
                        vā yavāgūr bhavatv iti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.65.40">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 6.65.40</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         yad anirdiṣṭaṃ buddhigamyan tad ūhyam |
                        <caesura/>
                         yathā abhihitam annapānavidhau caturvidham annapānaṃ bhakṣyaṃ
                        bhojyaṃ lehyaṃ peyam iti | evaṃ caturvidhe vaktavye dvividham
                        abhihitaṃ || atrohyaṃ bhavati annapāne viśiṣṭe dvayor grahaṇe
                        caturṇṇām api grahaṇaṃ bhavati ||
                        <caesura/>
                         kiñ cānyat anne bhakṣyam aviruddhaṃ ghanasādharmyāt | peye lehyaṃ
                        dravasādharmyāt | caturvidhas tv āhāraḥ praviralaḥ | prāyeṇa
                        dvividha eva | ato dvitvam prasiddham ity āha bhagavān
                        dhanvantariḥ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.65.41"/>
                    <l xml:id="SS.6.65.42"/>
                    <l xml:id="SS.6.65.43"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.66.1"> athāto doṣabhedavikalpam adhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ
                        || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.66.2"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.66.3">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 6.66.3</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         aṣṭāṅgāyurvedavidaṃ kāśirājam mahīpatiṃ |<cb/>
                        <caesura/>
                         cchinnaśāstrārthasandehaṃ sūkṣmāgādhamivodadhiṃ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.66.4">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 6.66.4</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         viśvāmitrasutaḥ śrīmāṃ suśrutaḥ paripṛcchati ||
                        <caesura/>
                         dviṣaṣṭirdoṣabhedā ye purastātparikīrttitāḥ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.66.5">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 6.66.5</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         kati tatraikaśo jñeyā viṃśo vāpy athavā triśaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         tasya<cb/> tad vacanaṃ śrutvā saṃśayacchinmahātapāḥ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.66.6">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 6.66.6</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         prītātmā nṛpaśārdūla suśrutāyāha tattvataḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         trayo doṣā dhātavaś ca pūrīśaṃ mūtram eva ca | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.66.7">

                        <caesura/>

                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.66.8ab">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 6.66.8ab</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         rogāṇāñ ca sahasraṃ yac chata viṃśatir eva ca | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.66.8cd"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.66.9">

                        <caesura/>
                         dviṣaṣṭidhā bhavanty ete bhūyiṣṭham iti niścayaḥ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.66.10">

                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.66.11">

                         tribhir pañcāśad etan tu sahaivaṃ kṣayam āgataiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         hīnamadhyādhikādvekakṣīṇavṛddhās tathāpare </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.66.12">

                        <caesura/>
                         dvādaśaiva samākhyātā rogayonir dviṣaṣṭidhā |
                        <caesura/>
                         miśrā dhātumalairaiva yānty asaṃkhyeyatām api | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.66.13">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 6.66.13</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tasmāt prasaṃgaṃ saṃyamya doṣabhedavikalpanaiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         rogaṃ viditvopacared rasabhedair yathe ritaiḥ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.66.14">

                        <caesura/>
                         kāryam ārogyam evaikam anārogyam athāpi vā | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.66.14a">

                        <caesura/>

                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.66.16">

                        <caesura/>

                <div type="colophon">

                    <head>[<foreign xml:lang="en">Colophon</foreign>]</head>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.66.colophon1">
                        <label xml:lang="en">6.66.colophon1</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         samāptañ cedaṃ sahottaratantram ity ato nighaṇṭur bhaviṣyati || ❈
                        || </l>


                    <l met="Sragdharā" xml:id="SS.6.66.colophon2">
                        <label xml:lang="en">6.66.colophon2</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         rājye śrīmānadeve pṛthusitayaśasi prodyadinduprakāśe
                        <caesura/>
                         kāle puṇyārjjanasya sakalajanamanohlādiramye vasante
                        <caesura/>
                         varṣe caikottare 'smiṃs tritayaśatagate mādhave māsi śukle
                        <caesura/>
                         saptamyāṃ puṣya ṛkṣe daśaśatakiraṇe vāsare siddhayoge |</l>

                    <l met="Sragdharā" xml:id="SS.6.66.colophon3">
                        <label xml:lang="en">6.66.colophon3</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         utpattyādyambuvelākulavividharujagrāhajuṣṭātiraudre
                        <caesura/>
                         saṃsāre sāgare 'smiñ jagad idam akhilaṃ glāninam sampravīkṣya
                        <caesura/>
                         tasmāc chrīharṣacandro niratiśayaghṛṇābhāvito moktukāmaḥ
                        <caesura/>
                         prītyā caigaṃ <sic>prākhilat</sic> suśrutākhyam |<anchor
                            n="SS.6.66.colophon3-n1"/>
                    </l>

                    <ab corresp="#SS.6.66.colophon3" type="apparatus">
                        <list type="Notes">
                            <item xml:lang="en" corresp="#SS.6.66.colophon3-n1">It is hard to understand how a word ending in
                                    <foreign>-gaṃ</foreign>, or any accusative, could
                                precede <foreign>prākhilat</foreign> or even <foreign>pra
                                    akhilan</foreign>. Some readers have emended <foreign
                                    xml:lang="sa">prākhilat</foreign> to <foreign
                                    xml:lang="sa">prālikhat</foreign>, a rare verb, but
                                one that at least governs the accusative. We do not see
                                metathesis elsewhere in the work of K's scribe, which is
                                generally very accurate, so we consider the emendation
                                unlikely. With so many words missing from this passage, we
                                consider that emendation is not useful.</item>

                            <item>We read <foreign>-harṣacandro</foreign> which could be
                                the name of the scribe. But the following
                                    <foreign>nnirati-</foreign> is hard to construe. If we
                                read the ablative <foreign>-harṣacandrān</foreign>, it
                                solve the problem of <foreign>-nn-</foreign> but is also
                                hard to construe.</item>
                        </list>
                    </ab>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.66.colophon4">
                        <label xml:lang="en">6.66.colophon4</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         śrīgaṇadevadevakuladūnī gvalakanivāsino vaidyavasuvarmaṇaḥ
                        pustakam idaṃ paṭhitvārtham avagamya sarvasattvānām upadeśaṃ
                        vidhātuṃ pratipāditam | atas tad ādhikrayābhyāṃ tad gotrajena
                        kenacin na kañcid dātavyam | yadā nopakriyate tadāsmān eva
                        pratyarpaṇīyam iti || </l>


                </div>
